 // Ad Block detection code per ticket AST-440
 ga('provide', 'adblockTracker', function(tracker) {
     // If we have already detected an ad blocker, then short-circuit
     if (adsBlocked) {
         sinclairDigitalAnalytics.customDimensions.dimension4 = "true";
         return;
     }
     var ad = document.createElement('ins');
     ad.className = 'AdSense';
     ad.style.display = 'block';
     ad.style.position = 'absolute';
     ad.style.top = '-1px';
     ad.style.height = '1px';
     document.body.appendChild(ad);
     adsBlocked = ad.clientHeight >0 ? adsBlocked : true; // If height < 1 then we assume a blocker
     document.body.removeChild(ad);
     sinclairDigitalAnalytics.customDimensions.dimension4 = adsBlocked ? "true" : "false"; // GA requires a string value
 });
 ga('provide', 'getPageType', function(tracker) {
     var path = window.location.pathname;
 
     if (path === "/") {
         // 'pathname' will not return any query string or hash, so this should work for all site types
         sinclairDigitalAnalytics.customDimensions.dimension6 = "home";
         return;
     }
     if (path.indexOf("/gallery/") >-1) {
         sinclairDigitalAnalytics.customDimensions.dimension6 = "gallery";
         return;
     }
     if (path.indexOf("/weather") === 0) {
         // Includes all subsections of /weather, per request
         sinclairDigitalAnalytics.customDimensions.dimension6 = "weather";
         return;
     }
     if (path.indexOf("/traffic") === 0) {
         // Includes all subsections of /traffic, per request
         sinclairDigitalAnalytics.customDimensions.dimension6 = "traffic";
         return;
     }
     if (path.indexOf("/watch") === 0) {
         // The News3 version of the Watch page uses this Head component instead of type_news_v3/head/v3
         sinclairDigitalAnalytics.customDimensions.dimension6 = "watch";
         return;
     }
 
     // All other sections should report as simply "section"
     sinclairDigitalAnalytics.customDimensions.dimension6 = "section";
 });

 ga('require', 'adblockTracker');
 ga('require', 'getPageType');
 ga('send', 'pageview', sinclairDigitalAnalytics.customDimensions);

   <script>
    function extractDomainFromUrl(fullUrl) {
     if (typeof fullUrl === 'string' && fullUrl != '') {
         var domainString = '';
         try {
             if (fullUrl.indexOf('://') >-1) {
                 fullUrl = fullUrl.split('://')[1];
             }
             fullUrl = fullUrl.split('/')[0];
             var domainArray = fullUrl.split('.');
             var domainPosition = domainArray.length - 2;
             var domainString = domainArray[domainPosition].toLowerCase();
         } catch(excp) {
         }
         return domainString;
     } else {
         return '';
     }
 }
 
 sinclairDigital.ast = sinclairDigital.ast || {};
 sinclairDigital.ast.referrerDomain = extractDomainFromUrl(document.referrer);
 
 if (sinclairDigital.ast.referrerDomain === extractDomainFromUrl(document.location.href)) {
     sinclairDigital.ast.referrerDomain = 'null'; // referral from self = 'null'
 }
 
 if (sinclairDigital.ast.referrerDomain === '') {
     sinclairDigital.ast.referrerDomain = 'false'; // unknown referrer = 'false'
 }
   </script>

          sinclairDigital.dependencies.define([],function(){
     function fetchWeather(zip) {
         var fetch = $.ajax({
             url: '/api/rest/audiencero/weather/zipcode/' + zip
         })
         return fetch;
     }
 
     function renderWeather(weatherZipCode) {
         fetchWeather(weatherZipCode).done(function(data){
             try {
                 var obj = {
                     weather: data.data[0]
                 }
                 $('.sd-weather-current-icon').removeClass('wi-stk-66').addClass('wi-stk-'+obj.weather.forecast.current.iconCode);
                 $('.sd-weather-current-temp').text(obj.weather.forecast.current.tempF);
                 $('.weather-current >.no-margin .wx-temp').text(obj.weather.forecast.current.tempF).append('<i class="wi wi-degrees"/>');
                 $('.wx-icon-text >.wx-icon >.wi').removeClass('wi-66').addClass('wi-'+obj.weather.forecast.current.iconCode);
                 $('.wx-icon-text >.wx-text').text(obj.weather.forecast.current.skyText);
                 $('.wx-container').css('opacity',1)
             } catch (e){
                 console.log(e)
             }
         })
     }
 
     $('#sd-desktop-search').on('keydown',function(){
         if($(this).val().length >= 3) {
             $(this).siblings('button').addClass('search-active');
         } else {
             $(this).siblings('button').removeClass('search-active');
         }
     })
 
     renderWeather('52402')
 
 },true)
         </script>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
    </div>

          <script>
           sinclairDigital.dependencies.define(['Swiper'],function(){
     $( "#swiper-sidebar_side_scrolling .swiper-slide a" ).each(function() {
         var url = $(this).attr('href');
         $(this).attr('href', url.substring(0, url.lastIndexOf('/')));
     })
     
     function sponsoredWindowResize(){
         var ww = $(window).width(),
             spv = 1;
             if (ww<1025) {
                 spv = 3
             }
             if (ww<900){
                 spv = 2
             }
             if (ww<625){
                 spv = 1
             }
         return spv;
     }
     
     function sendGaTrackingEvent(label){
         ga('send', 'event', {
             eventCategory: 'SponsoredWidget',
             eventAction: 'click',
             eventLabel: label
         });
     }
     
     var sponsoredSwiper = new Swiper ('#swiper-sidebar_side_scrolling', {
         slidesPerView: sponsoredWindowResize(),
         autoplay: 5000,
         spaceBetween: 10,
         nextButton: '#swiper-sidebar_side_scrolling .swiper-button-next',
         prevButton: '#swiper-sidebar_side_scrolling .swiper-button-prev',
     })
     
     $('[class*="sidebar_side_scrolling"] .swiper-button-prev').on('click', function() {
         sendGaTrackingEvent("PrevButton");
     });
     
     $('[class*="sidebar_side_scrolling"] .swiper-button-next').on('click', function() {
         sendGaTrackingEvent("NextButton");
     });
     
     $('[class*="sidebar_side_scrolling"] .swiper-slide a').on('click', function() {
         sendGaTrackingEvent($(this).attr('href'));
     });
     
 }, true);
          </script>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
